suffered death to bring us to ever lasting bliss.

There for in cristus person makithe the prophet a great lamentacion for the
great vnkynddenesse that he seethe in mankind and seythe thus.

Thou man for vanite thou stinkyste for thy rusty sin and there for j cry
and weep for thou haste on thy head a garlonde of flowers and j for the have
one of thorns thou haste on thy ho^des a ^eyre of white glouys and j for thy
have many blody wounds

Thou haste in thine arms spradde to lead karrollis and daunces and mine arms
for the be nay led on a tree with sharp naylus. Thou haste thy clothis pynched
small and my body for the is full of great walis And o thing greuith me most
of all thou settust not by my passion that ^ suffered full sore for thy sake
But with thine horrible swering thou vpbyoydeste me with many great othis by
mine head eyes arms nails sides wounds fete bones be mine heart and be my
passion that thou sholdiste do worship to thou doste great spite and repreue



we read in the gestis of to maynes that an Emperor sent a great man to a
land to be a justice and or he come there no man in that country could swear
no oath but ye and nay. but when this Justice come a monge hem he made the
people to swear one bokys in sessiones and yafe hem chargis and so the people
took ensample of this justice to swear as he and his men did be our lordis
passion sydys Arms nails face wounds blood heart and so forth and took hit
so in use that the common people swore as they deed.

Than on a day as the justice sat in his office and chargid the people there
come to fore him a fair woman clothid all in grene and brought a feyre child
in her lap all blody and all to martered his head all to pryckyd his face
disfigured his eyes out his arms brokyn his hondis smetyn thourghe his naylys
cut and his fete cut from his leggrs his sydis all to rent his bowels and
his her te drawn out of his body. Thanne seyde this woman to the Justice.
what are they worthy to have that have thus do to my child and he seyde they
were worthy to have death. Thanne said she thou and thyn men with your horible
othis have thus dismembered my sweet sone ihesu criste that am I modyr un to and
thus ye have taught all your country where fore thou shalt have thy own
don^e and so in sight of all the people the earth opened and the justice fill
down to hell. and than the people were sore a gaste and they left all soche
great othis and ded a mende her lives and so late us leave all our othis and
leave as criscen shul de do and reverence the passion of our lord ihesu criste
that was cause of our redemption be the which we shall come to ever lastyng
bliss that never shall have end.

Dm^ca palmaru^.
GOod frendis as ye know well yt this day is callid Palm sunday but for
because that the service of this day is long I will tell you shortly why hit
is callid Palm sunday as seint johan seyth our lord ihesu criste come to
Betanye where he seythe Venit ihesus beta^^a^ vbi lazarus fuit mortuus que^
resusuitauit. And there he raised lazar from death to live that hade ley.iiij.
days deed and this lazarus was brothir to mary mawdeleyne and to martha that
was a nothir suster. Thanne ihesus wyste that his passion was nyghe and took
Lazar with him and rydyng on an ass he come toward iherusalem. and when the
people herd there of the people went ayense him. Non propter ihesum tantum sed
vt lasarum videre^t quem resuscitauit a mortuis. Not only for ihesu but for to
see lazar that was resyn from de^he to live and also for to see criste and do
him worship Acceperu^t remos palmarum and sternebant in via. They took
branches of palm and other flowers and strawed in the wey a yense his coming
And sum sprade her clothis in the wey and song Benedictus qui venit in
nomine domini. Blessed be he that comythe in the name of our lord king of
israhel where for holy church makyth this day solemn procession in mind of
the procession yt was made ayense crist. and also joy and myrthe of our
resing from death to live that has leyne all this year in dedly syn. now y
trust to god that they be resyd to god leuyng And for angeles of heaven make
much joy of your rising out of syn And thus we take palm and flowers in
procession as they did and go in procession knelyng to the cross in the
worshi^ and mind of him that was done one the cross worshippyng and well
coming him with song in to the church as the people ded our lord in to the
cite of iherusalem

Thanne johan bellet askithe a question and seith that criste had the grettest
worship rydyng one the ass that ever he had in this world Tha^ why
worship we the cross and not the ass to this question he answerithe him
self and seyth that the worship of this world as Salamon said All is but a
vanite and naught and makithe to for get a man his god and him self There as
great tribulacione dissese and heaviness causithe a man to think of god and
^rye to him for socoure and help and to know him self And there for all
christian people should put a wey all worldely vanitees that bryngythe much
people to great my scheue and many to ever lastyng pain. we worship the
cross for hit was cause of our redemption and salvation and to bring us to
ever lastyng joy and bliss that we hopyn all to come to Thanne anon when
criste was come to the cite of iherusalem he went to the temple and drove out
all buyers and sellers that he fonnde there in and seyde Domus mea do mus
oracionia vocabitur My house is a house of preyouris and ye make hit a den of
theuys Thus our lord yafe all christian people en sample to leave byyng and
sellyng on the holy day and in special in church. A nothir hit is why hit is
callid palm sunday for be cause that palm be tokenythe victory where all
criste^ people should bear palm in processione in tokenyng that he had
foughten with the fend and has the victory of him be shryfte of mouth
satisfactione with deed mekely done his penance with great contricione in his
heart and in this wise overcome his gostly enemy the fend we read in the
gestis of romans y^ it was the manner sum time. that if there were any lord
that were rebel a yense the Emperor a none the Emperor would send sum
worthy knight with great pissa^ ^^ of people to that land and put hem down
and make hem sogettys to the Emperor of rome And when this knight had
done so. than should he be set in a ch^ re ^ray^d with clothys of gold in
the best wise and a branche of palm in his hand in tokenyng that he had the
victory and with great worship brought in to rome but when he come in to
any worthy cite tha^ there should stand one by him and beat him in the mouth
with a branche of olyue sayng thus Anotholites this is to sey kowe thy self
that is to understand though^ thou be great now and have the victory make
not to much of thy self for hit may fortuue a nothir time thou maiste have
the worse and turn to much vylony. more than now to worship. where for ^e
not now to proud of thy self.

Thus should ye beat your self in the mouth of your soul with the branche
of olyne that is with the virtue of meekness and so bold you in love and meke
in her te and ever more dreding and feryng left he fall a yene in to sin And
so leave the worship^ that ye have now. For trust this trewly ^^^knesse is that
virtue that most and so ^este over comes your gostely enemy the fend and
souneste gaderithe a man to vertuos leuyng that we may have this virtue of
meekness patience and charity to over come our gostly enemy now and ever Amen

GOod frendis ye shall understand that holy church vsid these three days and
seythe service in the euyntyde that is meekness where for we call hit
tenables. But holy church callid hit tenebras Than why this service is thus
done in mekeuesse holy fadres tellithe for three causis One is the night
before that our lord ihesu crist was take he went un to the mount of olyuete
and preyde thus Pater misipassibile est transeat a me calix iste My fadyr if it
be possible that this bitter passion may pass fro me if it were the fader is
will and else not And for dread and fere of that bitter passion that he field
in his sperit he sweet both blood and watyr A nothir cause is this that a no^
aftir myd night come judas with ^. knyghtis and much other people to take
criste and for hit was myrke and they could not well know him from seynte
james he was so like criste there for judas seyde Quem osculatus ^^ero ipsum
em^ tenete For sothe quod he him that I shall kiss it is take ye him for seint
james was so like criste that much people callid him cristus brothir and thus
judas be trayed his mastyr and thus was criste take in meekness with all the
spite that they cowde do to him beting him and spetyng in ^his face. The
thrydde cause is when criste was naked on the cross fete and hand hangyng
three ow rys from vnderyn till none Thanne the son with drowe her light and
was ^er^e thourghe all the world showing that the makyr of light was at that
time payned to death for these three causis the service in the night is done in
myrkenesse. the which service makyth mind how judas betrayed criste and how
jews come as preuely as they ^oude for dre de of the common people where for to
the service is no bell ronge but a sound made of tree where all christian p^eple
may have knoweliche to come to this service preuely with out making of any
noise and all that the people should speak of coming and going should sound of
the tree that is the cross that our lord was done upon and of his passion and
of the wordys that our^ lord spoke ha^gyng on the cross and howshe seyde to
his modyr Mulier ecce filins tuns w^man see thy son and how he commanded his
modyr to seint johan the evangelist in keeping and what seyde the these that
hyng by him and said thus. Domine ^nan^o v^neris in reg^um tuum memento me^.
Lord when thou comyste to thy kingdom have mind of me and a none our lord
said to him. Hodie me^umeris in paradiso. This day thonshalte be with me in
paradyse and how he took his spertte in to his faderis handis and seyde In
manus tu^s domine ^^. and so he yield up the ghost thus coming and going to the
church all christian people should common and leave vanite and ydill talkyng and
speak only to the cross that is o^^e redemption ^ no their cause is when that
^udas hadde^ be trayed tris^e and saw by his treson he should be deed ano^ he
fill in despair and honge him self on a tree and than he displesid more criste
for that deed tha^ for all the trespass that he had done to fore for criste is
so merciful that and he had asked mercy he hulde have had mercy and for
yeuenesse Also at this service is set certain can delis in the quere Aftyr
the use in sum place more than in some other as the use is the which be
quey^^hith one aftyr a nothir in tokenyng of cristis disciples how they went a
wey each aftyr other But when all these candelis be takyn a wey and the light
gone yet on a bidith still a while till clerkys have song keryes and these
^erses the which be tokenethe the wymmeu that made lamentacion at cristus
sepulcre Thanne that can ^^ll is brought ^ yene and other light there at that
be tokeneth on^e lady ^o: all the feythe was los^ save only our lady and of
her all other were informed and taught Also it be tokeneth criste him self
that was in his man hode deed and leyde in se ^^l^re and the thrydde day rose
from death to live a yene and yafe light beloue to all that where deed and
quente be despair The strokys that the priest yeuethe on the book be tokenithe
the clap^es of the thou^dye wha^ criste brake hell yatys and dispoyled hell
and fett^ out adam and eve and all that he had boughte with his pitter
passione Now have ye herd some what what this serui^^ be tokenithe and think
there upon and be not unkind to your lord god that suffered all this for
you for ^ukyndenesse is a sin that seynky^h in the sight o^ god. As seynte
Ambros seythe. that there may no man fy^de a pain great ynow to punysche
unkindness and that ye shall here be ensample.



I find that Alysau^dyr necham tellith how that there was sumtyme a knight
that went out of his own country fe^ in to a strange land to seek auentures
and hit hap pid he come in to a great foreste and there he her d^ a great noise
of a best that seemed in dispire and than he wolte wete what hit mente and
went ne re and saw how a gret^ horrible addy^ and of great lenghte be clippyd
a lion and bunde him to a tree as he lay and slepid and when the lion woke he
found him self bound and might not help him self ^e made a great horrible
noise de ^yryng help of the knight tha^ had this knight compassion on this
lion and would feign have help but he dradde wha^ he was lou se left he would
have fallyn to him but be cause he was knight and the lion was king of all
bestis in that distress he took his sword and smote addyr a sondy^ Than a
none the lion felt him self louse and fill down to the knyghtys fete and
ever aftyr night and day in every place he followed the knight and every night
the lion lay at this knyghtys beddis fete and in every battle the lion was
ready to help his maistre in so much that the people spoke to the knyte of the
lion yet be counsel of much people he had the lion in suspecte where for
wha^ he went in to his own country a yene p^uely while the lion sleppe he
took the watyr and went in to ship and seylid for the and when this lion
woke and myssid his ma^tyr a none he y^^e a great roryng and went aftyr him in
to the sea and swam aftyr him as he might and wha^ his might sailed thann he
was drowned. By this knight ye may understand goddis sone of heaven that come
out of far country that was out of heaven in to this world and was bound
for mankind with this old addyr the fend to a tree of in obed ience where for
with the sharp sword that was his passione he lousid mankyde out of his
boundis and made him fre to goo where he would And there for all christian people
be bou^dyn to worship him and thank him for his lousing and to be buxum to
him all the time that they leave and follow and sewe the lore of holy church And
he shall pass thourghe the watyr that is to sey thourgh the pain of death and
he shall come to the joy that ever shall last with outyn end the which god
bring us all to Amen

Diverse questions Any men wolle ask diverse questio^ns of the service of
these days of soche prystes that they suppose can not make no ready answer to.
but put him to shame and do to him vyloni and rep^uith where for I have te
telith which be needful for every priest to know and if he woll look hit ready
and keep hem ready in heart he may make ready answer and so shall hit be to him
both profit and worship. First if a man ask how she rethursday is callid
so* ye may sey that in holy church it is callid Ce^^ domini our lordis soper
day for that day ^e souped with his disciples opynly and aftyr souper he gafe
hem his flesche and his blood to ete and to drink and seyde thus. Accipite et
mand^ rate hoc est corpus meum Take ye this and ete it for hit is mine own body
and a none aftyr he woshe all his disciples fete showing what meekness that
was in him and for the great love y^ he had to hem It is also in englische
callid shere thursday for in old fadres days the people would that day shere
her head dis and clippe her berdis and do down her he dys and so make hem
honest a yene estyr day. for on good friday they do her bodies none ese but to
suffer penance in mind of him that that day suffered his passion for all
mankind. on Estyr even it was time to here her service and aftir service make
holy day.

Hit is wreton in the lyffe of a seynte that he was so besy on the saturday
before none that he made ^'man to shave him aftyr none than was the f^nde ready
and gaderyd us the heris than this h^ly man saw that and commanded him to tell
why he did so than seyde he thou doste no reverence to thy holy day therefore
wolle keep these heris till the day of dome in great rep^ue to the Than a non
he left of shauyng and took these heris from the fend and made to brenne hem
in his own hand to suffer penance and so a bode vnshauyn till mo^day aftyr
This is said to all tho in rep^ue that worship not the saturday at aftir
none. Than as Johan Bellet seithe on there thursday a man should do down his
head and clippyn his berde and a pryste should shave his crown so that there
should no thing be between god and him for heris come of superfluite of veins
and of humures of the stomach and they should pare her nails of hands and fete
that comythe of superfluite of fylthe with out forth and shryue hem and make
hem clean with in his soul as with out. And thus make him clean both with in
and with out The while that all this lenton has be drawyn between us and the
quere be tokenithe the passione that was hid and vnknowyn till the days come
the which these days be done a way ande the Auter opynly shewde to all the
people for these days criste suffered his passion opyniy that he had haugyng
on the cross. Consummatum est it is endid that is to sey. now the prophecy of
my passion has an end. where for the clothis of my auter be takyn a wey For
cristis clothis were takyn a wey from him. and so was done nakid on the cross
save as our lady his modyr wont a kercoffe about him to cover his membris.
The auter stone be tokenythe cristus body that was drawyn on the cross as a
skin of perch meant on a harow so that all his bonis might be told

The besemes that the auter is wechyn with be tokenythe the s^ourgys that they
betyn our lor dis body with and the thorns that he was crouned with The watyr
and the wine that it is waschyn with be tokenythe the blood and the watir that
ran down fro his woundis that was in his side peryshyd with a spear The wine
that is poured upon the auter on the v. crossis be tokenith the blood that
ran down from his principalle wondis of his body. Also this day is no paxe
yeuen at the mass for Judas be trayed crist this uyght with a cosse this was
the prophecy of his passion this day endid. where for this night wha^ he had
soupyd he made the sacrament of his own body and gaffe hit to his disciples to
ete and drink and began the sacrament of the mass and of the new law and
aftyr souper he wysche his disciples fete that was a manner of the new law
full out for as he seyde to Petyr he that is washin and is clean of dedely syn
has no need to be waschyn it be tokenythe the affliction of venial sins
Than if people ask why prystes do not mass aftyr fouper as criste deed It
was turned in to more honest and more saluacione to man's soul for as Hyamo
tellith upon the pistell of seint Poule that many in the beginning of the
feythe comythe to church on sherethurday and tho that were rich bryngithe
mete and drink with hem and eton and drynkyn her belyes full and than at
night tokyn her hosell and seyde that criste gafe hem ensample Lu^ when the
rich e^e and drink to much the pore people a bydythe with out till aftyr
the rich has done fore an hu^gerid and than eton of the releffe that they
left. and so aftyr the people took her hosell. where as the pistell of this
day tellithe. saint poule rebukithe hem there of and turned that foul use in
to more honest and clennes and holiness. that is for to sey mass fasting all
people to take her hosell fasting on estyr even the pascall is made the chief
tapir in the church So is criste chief above all the seyntis in heaven The
pascall also be tokenyth the pelour of light fere that went before moses and
the children of israhel when moses ladde hem out of Egipte in to the land of
be hefte that is Iherusalem and so they passid save and sound. And so vij.
days aftyr they come all in to these and thankyd god for her passage. And in
mind here of holy church vsithe all the Estyr woke to go a processione to
the founte that is now the reed see to all christian people that be cristened in
the fouute for the watyr in the founte be tokenythe the read see for blood and
watyr is the wou^des that were in cristus sydys in the which the power of
pha^^o the fend of hell is drowned and all his might lost and christian people
failed and for the founte is hallowed on Estyr even and one wytson even for in
the beginning all children a bode to be cristeued one these.ij. days and to be
cristoned at the founte halowyng But now for because that many in so long
abydyng were ded with out cristendome. where for holy church ordained now to
cristo^ all times of the year save viij. days before these evenys the child
shall abide to the founte halowyng if it may for parell of death and else not.

Thus is the paschall hallowed be light with new fire and of hit all othyr
taperis and candellis be light for all hoolynesse and good techyug and good
leuyng comythe of criste and techyng of holy church and lightithe hem in
cristus passione with brennyng love and charity Pecys of ensence he styckyde in
the paschall in the manner of a cross tho be tokenith the v. wounds of our
lord as Bede seythe that he suffered in his body that shall be frecsche and
sweet as any ensence till the day of dome to great rep^ue to all that shall be
dampened that believe not in cristis passion and woll not ask mercy and
foryenesse of her sins. In the founte halowyng the pryste cast watyr in the
iiij parties of the founte for crisce hade his disciples going prechyng and
techyng m four parties of cristome in the name of the fadyr and the sone and
the holy ghost

And aftir the pryste bre thithe one the watyr for the holy ghost in making of
the world was borne upon watres for when god for adames syn cursed the earth
and land. he cursed not the watyr* where for it is lawful to a man to ete in
lento^ that ^omythe of the watyr

Aftyr he dropythe the wex in to the watyr of a candell brennyng the which
betokenythe the ma^hode of criste that was fullyd in watyr and puttith oil and
creme in to the watyr for by the virtue of the sacrament tho that be in heaven
and in earth be joined to gedyr and that was preuyd be cristus baptyme for
there the fadyr of heaven spoke and seyde Hic est filin^ me^a dilectus in ^^^
michi been complacui This is my well-beloved sone that woll plese me. And the
holy ghost was seyne Sicut culumba As a white do ue thus was the fou^te
hallowed. ij. tyme^ in the year. At wytsontyde and at Estyr when all the people
is brought out of thraldom be cristus passion from the danger of the fend
and at wytsontyde for than is the holy ghost yeuen in remission of all sins.
Than from the founte the people gothe to the quere syngyng the latanye preyng
all the seyntys of heaven to prey to god to give to all that be cristyn to keep
that worthy sacrament to goddis plesaunce and the couenaunte that they have
made in her cristonyng. Than the priest gothe to the mass for criste that is
head of all holy church is not reason. kyrieleysou is seyde. for i^ every
preyoure in especial in the mass it is great need to ask help and so cour
of god to keep us from all manner of temptaciones that the fend puttith in us
and namely in goddis service Gloria in excelsia is seid for the fadyr of heuyne
has great joy to be hold the people that his so ne has boughte with his
passione and to see hem in rest pese and charity echone with other. The greyle
is not seyde for tho that be few cristoned be not yet perfect to walk in
grace of ^tuous Alleluya is said for it is great joy to angeles to se be
cristonyng the nombre of hem restored a yene Aftyr alleluya a tracte is seyde
hey songen for though be cristonyng they be wasche from synyit must the
travel besely to keep hem from co^beraunce of the fend that they fall not in
dedly syn The offertory is seyde for the wyme^n that come^ with oyntementys to
offer to cristis body they found him not in his to^ be Agnus dei is seyde but
no pax give for criste that is head of pes is not yet reason The post common is
not seyde for tho that be new cristoned should not be hoseled this day but on
the morrow for in old time there come to cristonyng people of great age Than a
short euynsonge is done for the children that were not cristoned. where of
gretely they where noyed with sickness of cold of long service thanne is
endid under a short Colet of all the sacrament of cristonyng is endid in the
passione of Criste by the which all christian people were restored to ever
lastyng bliss to the which god bring us all to Amen.

In die paraschene.
GOod frendis this day is callid god friday for all that our lord ihe su criste
suffered this day turned us to great joy for this day he suffered passione
vndyr pounce pylate fore our sake Hit is an old say that a foul be gynuyng
has a foul endyng. Now se how this pylat be ganne cursidly and endyd full
wrechidly for as seynte Austen seythe cursed leuyng furste askith a cursed end
aftyr he that for getith him self here in his leuyng is full like to for get
himself in his last end.

This pylat was a knights sone that was callid Tyrus that gate him of a woman
that hyghte Pyle and this woman nes fadyr hyghte at. so when this child
was borne they set the moderys name and the gru^de fadyr after and so by
both names callid him Pylat Than after when he was of.iij. year of age his
modyr brought him in to the knights court to his fadyr Than had the knight a
nothir sone ny like to pylates age but for this knyghtys so ne was in all his
reule more gentillere more manfully more godly more beloved than this pylate.
so for hate and for enuy^ there of this pylat one a day slew this knyghtys
sone than was the knight wondyr sorry but yet he would not sle pylat aut sent
him to rome to be there in hostage for a tribute that the knyt should pay to
the emperor Thanne hit happid that the king of france had sent his sone
thedir for the same cause Thanne for be cause when pylate saw that he was more
beloved and cherisched and than this pilate slew him Than for he was so cursid
the emperor be counsel of the romans sent pylate in to a country that was
callid pounce where that the people of that country were so cursid that they
slew any that come to be maystre over hem So when this pilate come thethir he
applied him to her maneres so what with wyles and sotilte he overcome hem and
had the maystry and gate his name and was callid pylate of pounce and had great
domynacion and power Thanne the king of iherusalem sent aftyr him and made him
leave tenant vndyr him of the lond^^ of jury And for pilate lyked well the
office preuely he sent to the Emperor and had his office confermed of him
vnwetyng to the king herod king that time where fore when king herod herd
what he had done he was so wroth and they were enemies un to the time that
our lord ihesu criste was take and thanne they be come fren disayene and fill
both in to one assent of cristis death. Thanne happyd hit aftyrwarde that the
Emperor fill sike and sent aftyr criste fore to hele him for hit was told
him that criste helid all that ever would come to him of all manner of
sykenesse what sum ever sykenesse hit had be But thanne had pylate done him
to death or the messengere come Than when the Emperor understand that he
sent for pylate and made him come to him. and when pilate herd^ this he was
sore a ferde and took one Cristus cote^* And so when he come to rome to the
Emperor All tho that were in present made pylate good chere all the while
that he had on Cristus cote And the emperor swore be fore that he should be
deed. Than took they of the cote and a none as the cote was of the Emperor was
so w^othe with pilate that he put him in to a prison till he had take
counsel what death that he should dye on. Than as soon as pylate woste and
understand that he should be deed he took his own knyfe and slew himself
with all. And when the Emperor herd there of and understand that he had
slain him self and thanne a none he made to teye a great stone a bowte
pylates neck and to cast him in to a watyr that is callid Tybir thanne when
he was cast in there the fendis made soche a noise there a boute that all the
Cite of rome was sore a freyed of hem.

Thanne when the Emperor saw this he made to take him up ayene and than was
he cast in to a watyr that was betwixe to hye hills and sollonge time astyr
there was in the watyr many horrible sightes said a bowte that cursed man.

Thus our lord ihrsu criste suffered passion and death for all mankind and
furste when he was take they did buffete him and stripyd him naked and beat
him with stourgis A vertice capitia vs^ ad plantis pedmn non fuit in eo sanitas
that fro the highheste place of his he de to the sole of the fete was no thing
left hole one him but all raw and aftyr made a croune of thornys and set hit
on his head and beat hit down with st^^ys of reed that hit perischyd his
brain and when they had peyned him so they lad de him forth all blody
Admontem cal^arie. To the mount of calnarye to the end of death yet wymmen of
the Cite when they sighe him so foul fare with and all to luggi^ and to draw
for very pit they wept upon him. Tha^ seyde our lord to hem Nolite flere
super me sz super vos et filios vestros. ye wymmen of iherusale^ weep ye not
for me but upon you and your children. for there shall days come in the
which ye shall bliss the wombes that were bareyne and the pappys that never
gave socke. Thus our lord preached be fore the vengeance that fill aftyr upon
iherusalem. The which prophecye Jeremye the prophet spoke of that is radde in
holy church these three days at tenebras the which was so horible of many
diverse myscheuys and in special of hou^ger that children lay for hounger deed
in the stretis Than was there a woman was come of great birthe that for hunger
took her own child that fed with her pappys and slew hit and partid hit in
ij. parties and than she rostyd half and that other half she kept till on
the morrow. Thanne as people come by the street they had sauoure of the roast
and anon they come in to have had part there of and when they saw the modyr
roste her own child and sone they were heavy and foul dismayed and would notte
ete there of but went their wey forth ayene. Than took the modyr of that
child and ete there of and seyde in this manner wise this is mine own sone and
mine own child that I bare of my body and fed hit with my pappys but yet I
wolle rathir ete hit than dye for hunger There for I tell yew this for to show
yew somewhat of the vengeance that fill in the cite of iherusalem aftir the
death of our lord ihesu criste Thanne they ladde him to the mount of Caluarye
and there they s^reyned so on the cross that every bone of his body might be
known on from a nothir and naylyd him hand and fete to the cross and they
gave up the cross and the body to gedyr and with a great peyse they let the
cross and the body fall down to gedir in to the morteyse that all the body
dasch^d and all his bones crakyd and his joints braste and ^eynes and all
wou^des braste out of blood sydis arms legs fete and bonds so that there
left no blood in him And ^^^ they took a clothe wlyle the blood was hot and
wonde hit a boute his body till the blood was cold and than they drew away the
clothe and pullid away the flesche from the bones this was a great pite. And so
when he should dye he began as Johan Hellet seythe. Deus meus respice in me And
so seyde all verses sewyng till he come un to that verse. In te domine speram.
And so at this verse An manus tuas domine commendo spiritum meum redemisti me
domine deus veritatis. There he gave up the spirit This is a great ensample
that our lord ihesu Criste ^n to all christian that every man should have in
mind these verses And he that can hem s^y and if he sey hem ^uery day he shall
not dye no manner myscheuous nor rengeable death. Thann^ aftyr this passi on we
sey orysons and knelyng at every orison save at that orison that is seyde for
the iewis at that orison holy church knelith not for be cause jew ysm scorn
knelyng three times to criste wha^ they scourgid him Thanne these orisones holy
church preyith for all manner of people for iewis sarise nes cysmatys heretikis
but not for christian people for while any man or woman stonte a cursed he is
dampened be fore god and dampened shall be at his death but he repent him and
amend him while he leuith in this p^sente world But take he de what seint
Auste^ seith Siscirem pro certo^nod ^ater meus esset in in^erno non ^r arem pro
illo nisipro diabolo. if I wyste for a truth that my fadir were dampened in to
hell I would never prey for him but as for the deuell of hell. for there is no
preyoure of holy church that helpithe a dampened man. Than aftyr these orisones
the cross is brought forth to the which all christian people should worship
this day in worship of him that this day dyed on the cross and to prey to
our lord ihesu criste to for give us all our tree space as criste preyde to
his fadyr of heaven to for give hem that ded him on the cross



There was a knight sum time and that was a great lord and he has a worthy
man un to his sone. And so hit hapyd that a nothir knight and this man fille
at debate and so this knight slew him. where fore the fadyr of this man
that was deed gade ryd a great multitude of people and pursewed that other
knight where so ener he went to have sleyne him night and day so that he
might have no rest but ever de de fley for fere of his lyffe. Thanne hit
happyd on a good friday this knight saw all christian people go to the church
And he be thought him that criste dyed that day on the cross for all man kind
and put him only in the mercy of almighty god and went to the church with
other people to serve god and when he was in the church a non this other
knight had word and come with much people in to the church and his sword
drawn in his ho^de for to sle him and wha^ this other knight saw that and
wyste well that he had trespased him and fill down flat to the ground
with his arms spradde a broad as our lord ihe su crist sprad de his armies on
the cross and seyde. For his love that this day sprad de his armies on the ercss^
and suffered passion and dyed for the and me and all mankind have thou mercy
one me and for give me thy sons death.

Thanne this knight thought hit had be to horrible a thing to smite him
while that he lay so and cried him mercy so mekely and a none he put up his
sword and seyde to him Now for his soue that this day dyed on the cross for
the and me and all m^^yn de I for give the and to ke him up and kyssed him and
a none went to gedyr aftyr un to do worship to the cross knelyng And when
this knight word have kyssed the fete of the cross the Image low sid his
armies from the crosset be clippyd the knight a boute the neck and kyssyd him
and spal e thus that all the people herd I for give the as thou haste fore
yeuen fore the love of me. and thus all christian people should do. and than they
should have mercy and grace of god and bliss ever lastyng.

In die pashe
GOod frendis ye shall know well that this day is callid in many places god
dis sunday ye know well that hit is the manner in every place of worshipp^ as
this day to do the fire out of the halle and the black wyntyr brandis and all
thing that is foul with smoke shall be done a wey and there as the fire was
shall be gayly arayde with fair flowers and s^rawed with grene ryschys all a
boute showing a great ensample to all christian people. Iyke as they make clent
her houses to the sight of the people in the same wise ye should cleanse you re
souls doing a wey the foul brennyng sin of lechery put all these a wey
and cast out all this foully smoky doste and straw in your souls flures of
feythe and charity and thus make your souls abyll to receive your lord god at
the feste of Estyr. Deponentes omnem maliciam

And put a wey all malice and all sorrow for right as ye wolle suffer no
thing in your house y^ stinkythe and saueryd ille where with ye may be
disceyued Night so criste when he comyth in to the house of your souls and he
find there any s^ynche of wrath envy or any other dedly sin he wolle not a
bide there but a none he gothe his wey and than comythe the fend in and
bydithe there. Thanne may that soul be sorry that is so for sakyn of god and be
take to the feude. Thus it is with tho that been in wrath and envy or in any
dedly sin and woll not for give to hem that has trespased to hem for no
preyoure he shall no for geuencsse have. foroure lord seythe thus. Dimittite
et dimit temini* For give and ye shall have for geuenesse. And there for every
christian man and woman should search well his conscience and make him abyll to
receive his savior ihesu criste very god and man.



There was sum time an holy bishop that preyde often besyly to god that he
might have grace to see and know which were worthy to receive that holy
sacrament and come to goddisbo^d Than on a time as he should hosell the people
he saw some come with her faces as read as blood and blood dropyd out of her
mouthis and sum her ^^^es when ^^ as b^a he as any py^he and s^mme were fay^^
and r^^d and lasty to ^e hot and sum as bryghte as ^^y snow Than among all
he saw ij. common wymen come and there faces shone as bryghte as the fone than
had the bishop great marvel of that sight and preyde to god to give him
reuelacion to wete what all this be tokenyd than there come to him an angel and
seyde tho that have blody faces and blood dropithe out of her mouthy be
enu^ous people and wrathful and woll not amend hem there of and ever they be
back bytyng and sclandryng her nepburis and be ever ready to swe^e o this there
for her mouthis shall drope black blood till they come to amendment and tho
that have black faces as pyche be lecherous and wolle not leave her syn and be
g^^t^ sinners in many de grees and* woll not ame^ ^ hem. They that have her
faces ^^ white as any ^nowethe fe be they that hau^e do great sin and be
shryuen there of and be sorry for her sins for the wypyng of her yen had
wa^chyd her souls and made hem clean and so they be in clean lyffe and trewly
labor for her leuyng. And tho ij. common wymen that shine so bryghte passing
all other they were great sinners and were sore a fer de whann e they come to
church and took a great repentance in her herti^ that they made a vow to god
preyng him hertely to fake no vetigeau^^e on hem and they would for sake her
sin and never do a mysse more where for god of his great gra^e and mercy
has for given hem her trespace and all her sins and the sorrow of her hertis
has so waschin her soulis that they shine so bryghte all other and than the
angel went his wey and the bishop kuelyd down and thankid god for his
reuelacion. And there fore take ensample ye this ij^ common wymen and be fory for
your sins and repe^te yew in your heart is purpose never to turn aye^ to
sin. And tha^ trustithe verily ye shall have grace and mercy and so coure to
ever lasting joy and blys* where for take this ^ certain though ye make hit
glofing with worcester des for to disceyue your gostly fadir and sey that ye be in
charity and be not. ye be gyle your self and trustid trewly ye shall not be
gyle god that sees every corner of your hertis. And there for disceue not
your ^^ne sowtes for the love of god and be as besy to make your souls clean
to the fight of god as ye be to make your houses to the sight of man. And as
ye would array yew in your best cle this that ye have a yense the coming of
your best frendis so should ye array ^o^^ now to ^^^e^ ^^e your best friend
that is your makir our lord ihesu crist that this time suffered passion and
de the to bring us to ever lasting lyff. This day is callid also a passing day
and in special for. ij causis One is for this day all criste^ people in

It is also a passing day for this day should all god dis children pass out of

GOod frendis these iij. days that is to sey mo^day tewis^ay and wedenesday ye
shall fast and go in p^ocellion man woman and servants for all we be sinners
and hauenede to prey to god for help grace and mercy for they may not excuse

self from the commandment of holy church wylfully he synnethe full
grievously Furste he synneth in pride for he is vnbuxum also synneth in slewthe
that knowithe him self in sin and woll not do his diligence to come out
there of. and right as he with drawid him from the people that beu gaderid to
serve god right so woll god put him from all the company of heaven and from
all the preyoures that be done in holy church till he come to amendment
There for all christian people come holly to gedyr and prey these iij. days to
all the seyntes in heaven to prey to god for us for we have sinned many times in
the year a yenste the commandment of god end there for these iij. days we
shall fast and prey to god of mercy and remission of our sins and put a
wey all the power of the fend and keep us from all myscheuous parell and
dredys that fallyn this time of the year more than any other time for in this
time many great thunderis and lightenyng. And as Lincolniences seythe. there
were fendis that fleteryn in the air for fere of the blaste of thundyr when
that criste come to the hell yates when he dispoyled hell and so yet when they
here the thundyr in the air they be so agaste there of that they fallen downd
and than go they not up ayene till they have do sum ^u^ sed dedis. for than
they rere wederys and make tempestis in the sea and draw down shippis and
make debate among the people and make on to sle a nothir and tend / fire and
brenne houses and draw down steples and trees and cause wymen to ouerley her
children and make people to hang he^ self and drown hem self in wanne hope
and in dyspeyre and do many cursed dedis. And for to put awey all soch my
scheuys and the power of the fend holy church has ordained that all
christian people shall fast and go a processione these three days and prey to
god and to our lady and to all seyntes of heaven of help and socoure. where
for in these processiones bellis be ro^ge baneres be splaed the cross comythe
aftyr and the people sewith aftyr. ^^r right as a king wha^ he gothe to a

the baneres comyth aftyr Than comyth the cross in cristus lykenes as king of
