Ascensio dm^
GOod friend is so che a day ye shall have an high and a solemn feste in
holy church that is callid the ascension of our lord the su Criste for that
day as the feythe and be leave techith how god is very god and man and styed up
in to heaven where fore in tokenyng of this the paschpll that is the chief
light in holy church that has sto^de openly in the quere from Estyr un to
this day Now hit is remeuyd a wey in tokening that criste is chief light in
holy church and so our lord diverse times openly apperithe to his disciples
and taught hem the feythe and the believe and this day hestyghed up in to heaven
and there wolle a ^y^e un to the day of dome. But now ye shall here the manner
of this ascension from escyr day unto this day he was not with his disciples
algates but diverse times appeared un to hem and he appeared to hem as they satyn
at her mete and ete with hem to show he^ that he was very god and man in
flesche and blood as they were For sum of hem they were in dowte left he
had be a spirit that has no(...) flecsche nor blood and there for to preue
the trowthe he ete with hem in her sight and badde hem go^ in to the hill of
olyue. and there in fight of all his disciples he blessed hem and styed up in
to heaven and left the steps of his fete thirst down in to the hard
marbull stone for a tokyn of his asce^sion Thanne ye shall understand that the
hill of olyuete be tokenithe merry where for criste styed up at the hill of
olyuete showing well that he is the head of mercy and he is ever ready to give
mercy to all that askithe mercy with meke heart. Thanne in his up rising as we
call Ascension angeles made so much melodye that no tongue may tell it so feign
they were of his coming Ascen dit velociter he styed up swyftely for as it were
a moment he was from earth to heaven A great clerk a philosouer y^ is callid
^abymoyses he seyth that it is as fer from earth to heaven as a holy man might
leave a thousand year and every day go a thousand mile. But he that met this
wey knowithe best. and this wey shall be met of a ryghtfull and a good man.
Thanne in his ascension he had with him a great multitude of fowls the which
he f^tte out of hell from the fendes bonds He styed up al so with his wounds
read fresche and blody And as bede seythe for v. causes. Furste for to very fie
the feyth of his resur rection for he wse in very flesche and blood that dyed
on the cross for all mankind. The secounde to show his wounds to his fadyr
in great help and socoure to all mankind. The thridde is to show how
ryghtfull they be da^ pned that woll not bele ue in his passion and in his
resurrection The four the isto show how merciful he is to them that woll be
leave and ask mercy. The.v. is that he bare with him a sign of victory for a
sykernesse to all mankind for like as a lord is siker that ha the a true
aduoket be for a Auge to answer fore him so in sikernesse to all mankind we
find him our aduket ener more ready to answer for us at thing that the fend
ou re gof^ly enemy makyth a yense us. where for seith the holy scripture a sike
rer attorney may no man be but god. Dbi matter oste^dit fill io pe ct as et
vhera. where for the modir showed the sone here breasts and her pappes Filius
patri latus et vulnera

The sone shewde to the fadyr his fides all to beto^ and his wounds bledyng
how should any thing be put a wey or deuydyd there as soch tokenes of love be
showed he may not fare a mysse that has soch to friend is in the country of
heaven Also by the steyng up in to heaven of our lord ihesu criste man has
gotyn a great dig^^te for a man to see his own kind and his own flesch and
hisblode sittyng on the right side of the fadyr of heaven in his trone where
for Angelus conderyng the dignite of man they would not suffer no man to do he^
worshipp^ ^^ they deed be fore the in ^^^^acion of our lord ihesu criste but
they worship men for god himself has take mankind on him and is now in
heuene bodily. Here by may a man see how much he is be hold to his god that
we where bound be fore and therll to the fend of hell and now we be made fre
of all that. and our lord ihesu criste has give un to man a fredome a bo^e
any Angeles. And there fore we be bound to him to do him service reverence and
worship. And there as Angeles sommetyme kepton the gatis of paradyse with
brennyng swerdis that no soul might come in. Now by feythe our lord ithesu
criste to mankind he has cast up the gatis and warn no man to enter there
in that is of stede^asee believe for as seynte Austeyn seythe. Apperuisti
credentibus regna celdr^n Thou hasee opened the gatis of heaven to them that be
leave

Also ye shall be leave right as a king of this world has in his country
officeris of diverse de grees sum higher and sum lower and sum more
preuyer thanne sum. So our lords steyng up at this time the lower Angel
for great woundre that they had in cristus Ascensione when they saw him in
flesche and blood steyng up to heuene with so great multitude of fo^les with
him And also for the great woundre that they had when they saw the fendes
of the air fly a wey for dread and fere of his sc^onge coming that be fore
were wont sparyng no thing to assail the souls that come by them and thanne
they flow^ fore great fece of this coming. Also the good Angeles come in all
the haste that they might to do our lord the sucriste service reverence and
worship. Thus for great woundre that the lower angel had of his freyng up
they asked the higher angel and they seyde. Quis est iste qui venit de edom
what is this that comythe out of the world with blody clothys as he were a king
of joy. This is he that with death sufferyng ready in his stour gyng sike and
deed in the cross strong in hell bodily in doing ferfull in rising and thus
has over come all his en myes and now is king glorious in heaven.

Thanne when our lord thesu criste was sty ed up in to heaven and than his
disciples stondyng with his modyr for great woundre of that sight and also of
the me lodye that they herd in the air they lokyd up in to heaven and suddenly
ij. Angeles clothid all in white stowde by hem and seyde. Diri galilei qui
statis aspicientes in celum hi^ est ihesus qui assu^ptus est a vobis.

Men of gelilee what sto^ de ye be holdyn in to heaven it is Ahesus that is
styed up from you and so he shall come at the day of dome a yene and deem all
quycke and deed

And there for all christian people lift up you re hertis to our lord ^he su
criste that now is styed up in to heuene and s^^tythe at his fadir right hand
and is ready to give mercy to all them that woll ask mercy with a meke heart.

And here fore there is no manner a man that may excuse him self nor have no
manner excusacion but if that woll himself and ask mercy to his lord god with
a meke heart and he shall have mercy and shall be sauyd ^^^ though a m^an be
never so sinful and he woll ask mercy with a meke heart he wolle give him
mercy. For contritu^et humiliatum deus non despiciea. A meke and a contrite her
te god shall never despice for and he wolle ask mercy and be sorry for his
sins our lord wolle take him to his mercy. Thanne for to show his great
goodness and compassion that our lord ha the of mankind A shall tell you
this ensample.



we read in the syffe of seinte Carpe how a man of mysse believe turnyd a
christian man out of his feythe and for soke his believe and his cristendo me
where fore this holy man Carpe was so wroth that he fill in great sykenesse
and when he shul de have preyde to god for a mendement he preyde night and day
that he might see hem have a bodily vengeance Tha^ hit happid at a
mydenyghte as he preyde thus suddenly the house that he lay ynne cleuyd in four
partis And he looked up and saw one honged so piteusly that hit was great pite
to se and than he lokyd up to heaven and there he saw our lord ihesu Criste
with a great multitude of angeles sittyng in his trone. and he lokyd up again
and than he saw this ij. men stondyng be fore an hot te ouyn quakyng and
tremelyng for dread of fend is like adderis and worms coming out of the ouyn
to draw the se ij. men in to the ouyn with hem. And so many other fendis come
in diverse likeness to help that they were into the ouyn Thanne was this holy
man Carpe feign to see these ij. men have that vengeance and was wou^ dre
glad there of that he lost the sight of our lord thesu criste and his
holy angelis for his heart was all one these ij. me^nes vengeance and was
sorry for it was so long or they were put un to her pain And than he rose and
went to him self and halpe all that ever he might and wha^ they were in to
the ouyn than was this Carpe very glad there of And than he lokyd up in to
heaven and there he saw our lord Jhesu criste and he saw him rise from his
trone for great pit and compassione that he had on the too men and come
down to hem and took hem out of her pain and seyde thus to Carpe Extend
manus tuas contra me Streche forth thine hondys ayense me and seyde thus I am
ready and need were to dye ayene for mankind rathir than to lose him.

^e this ensample ye may see how ready that our lord ihesu criste is to all
that wolle ask mercy and for yeuenesse and deserve mercy that is that every
man a mende and leave his sins and be in full will and purpose to sin no
more and thus he shall come to the grace and mercy of our lord ihesu criste
that suffered for us and all man kind one good friday and this day styed up to
heuene the which he woll grant us and bring us all there to Amen

Sequitur vigilia penthecosten


GOod frendis as ye know well a saturday neste coming is wydsonueuyn and ye
shall fast and come to chirch to here your service and make you ^^ene to
receive the holy ghost that the fadir of heaven sendithe among mankind where
for I counsel you and charge you if there be any of you that fall to any sin
that he come and amend him there of and I woll be ready to all that lo^gith to
me For take this in certain in the same wise as a man woll not go to a place
there as a stynckyng ^areyne is but if that he stop his nose and high him
thense. Right so the holy ghost flethe from the soul that is comberid with
dedely sin and angelus woll stop her nosys for much more fowler stinkith
dedely sin in the sight of god thanne does any careyn to smell to the people
and as the holy ghost fleth to hem that bydith in good lyffe and clean and in
parfyte love and charity and has pit and compassione of alletho that be in
any dissese or tribulacion to soch the holy ghost visitithe and comyth to. And
with soche as him listith to come to a bide and com(...)th and techith hem ^^
all need But as the service of this feste is more preysed than any othyr time
for as this feste holy church callith to hem and seythe Deni sancte spiritus.
Come holy ghost specially to have help and socoure and grace and to have part
of the dole that he makithe at this time to all christian people that be abell
to receive his yiftes. But ye shall understand that the holy ghost makith his
dole in other wise than other people. For they dele as hit likith he^ but the
holy ghost delithe to all the people that is needful and spedfull to hem that
y^^te and sum more and sum less one yifte and sum anothir some he yeuith
wisdom in holy scripture to understand holy scripture he yeuith grace to
have great lust and lykyng there ynne that is for to sey they be lusty to
preche and to teache virtue and goodness and e^ form the people to the hele of
their souls unto them that here hit and bear hit awey. But many had lever to
here a song of robynhode or tale of rebaudry where for goddis word shall not
be p^chith to soche. And sum he yeuithe grace so in understanding of diverse
langage As Englische French walche Irische with out any great travail in
lernyng hit is a great yifte and a miracle and a special grace of almighty god
that any man can understand our in spekyng There be v. letteres that makythe
all the words of all the world and of all langages that be under heuene. And
with out one of these letteres may no manner a man make no word and that been
these (...) A E I ^ and D*

And also sum he yeuithe grace of counsel for to do aftyr good counsel And
sum he enspirith with ynn for they that he shewith hem and makith them to
know to fore what woll come aftyr and fall And ye^ithe hem grace to de^e the
better from the worcester se where for they do so wisely and discretly that all the
people be glad to here hem speak and to do aftyr her counsel.

And sum he yeuithe grace also to do aftir co^sell as our lord ihesu criste
gave him self counsellyng a man that would leave a parfyte lyffe to leave all
that he has and go in to a religion and be there governed by his wardeynes
counsel and by his own this counsel comyth of god And sum he ^^^th also
grate of sufferyng much bodily sykenesse gr^te wrongs and much dissese both
in body and in soul loss of catell lordeshippes mastershippes frendis and all
that he sufferithe with a meke heart thankyng almighty god of his sonde this
comyth of the grace of the holy ghost. Also he yeuithe sum grace of lernyng
in diverse science sum to learn one craft and sum anothir so be ^he which
he may get his luyng with troth so th^^ a man woll put to hi^ good will and
his dilgence and trewly to labor and not to slo^^ ^^e and sleep slew the fuly
and unthrifty but ^ dew time to labor bes^ly the holy ghost has y^uen every
man somm^ knowing to get his luyng with truth. Also sum he geuythe grace
of pite and fills her hertes so full of pit^ and compassion of her euene
christian that he in dissese and aduersite that they yeuen hem of their goodis to
help and to socoure hem at her ^^de and to comfort^ hem in all that they may
for cristus sake and also mercyable that they for give hem all that they have
trespased to hem in any wise. Sum he yeuithe also to d^^de god in so much
that they be ever a fe^de to displese almighty god and ever thynke^ of great
vengeance that god woll take for sin at the day of dome Tim^r domini
expellit peccatum. the dread of god and the horrible peynes of hell puttithe a
wey sin and thus nyghthe and day sum be ever a ferde to offend god and
ever besely to do well in preuyte as in opyn sight of people he that has
this yifte has a special grace of the holy ghost. Her sunt septem do na
spiritua sancti. These be the yeftes that, the holy ghost departid among all
mankind and yeuithe sum more than sum But there may no man excuse him but
that the holy ghost ^assignithe him somewhat of these in time of his cristonyng
where the bishopp^ at the confermacion rehersithe these words of the sacrament
I woll tell you an ensample to fere you the more to the sacrament of cristonyng
that is fou^den in the lysse of seynte James



There was an holy bishop that turned low is the king of France to christian
feythe and so when the king come to christian at the halowyng of the founte there
was great prese of people that the clerk that bare the bishops crismatory
might not bring hit to the bishop. and so when the font was hallowed and
come to the Anoyntyng he might not come to his crismatory. tha^ the bishop
lift up his eyes to god preyng god deuontly for help and a none there with
there come a done as white as any milk that was the holy ghost beryng in her
bill a violl with oil and creme to the bishop And when he opened the vyoll
there come out there of so sweet a savor that all the people had wo^dre there
of and were greatly comfortid there by and that co^tynued till the service was
done. Here by ye may well se though the priest sey the wordis the holy ghost
worchith the sacrament and does virtue of the words.

Now that the holy ghost may descend and lyghten in us that we may come to
receive him to our saluacione Amen.

In die penthecosten


GOod men and wymmen this day is callid wit sunday for be cause that this day
the holy ghost brought wit and wisdom in to cristus disciples. and so by
her prechyng aftyr in to all cristendome Than may ye understand that many
has wit but not wisdom for there be many that have wit to p^che well
and to sey well but there be few that has wisdom to do well There be many
wise p^chorys and techourys. but her leuyng is no manner thing aftyr her
prechyng. Also there be many that labourith to have wit and connyng but few
trauelith to come to good leuyng for who so have wytte^ and connyng to get
good with fair sotyll wordis be they never so false he is wise but wit of
holiness is not set by For he that can get good falsely with knackys and
mowus he is a wise man but he that for sakyth the wit of this world is ^
sole But look what holy scripture seythe Dominus recitauit nom^ pa^peris quia
ipsu^ approbauit et nome^ eins in libro scriptum fuit Our lord has received
the name of the poor man for he has preuyd him in his pouerte and wretyn his
name in the book of lyffe

Sed nomen diuitia tacuit quia ipsu^ no^ approbauit. But he left the rich man
for he has not preuyd him but thoug^^ a man be never so rich at the last
he shall be pore For naught he bryngythe with him but his good dedis and his
badde he that leuythe well and techithe well for a good ensample in leuyng is a
good doctrine. This grace as this day was yeuen to cristus disciples for they
taught well and leuyd well for they gave good informacion ^^ techyng of good
ensample in leuyng sore her techyng and her leuyng is sprad de a bowte in all
the world. Than how the come to this grace ye shall here Post ascensioneml
domini. Aftyr when that our lord ihesu criste was steyed up in to heaven his
disciples were in great heaviness and morning for they had de lost her maystre
that they louyd full well and for him had de lost all there goodys for his love
and for sake all her frenchipp^ and sewed him full pore in hope that they
should gretely be helped by him. And thus they were all heavy and gretely
stonyed and sore a ferde to be takyn of the ie^o es and cast in prison and
aftyr to be put to death

This made hem sorry that they durst not go a monge the people sore to get hem
mete and drink* but yet as criste badde hem in his ascension they went in to
the Cite of Iherusaleth and there they were in an halle of stage and there they
satte to gedyr preyng un to god with hole heart and one sperite of help and
socoure and sum comfort in her dissese Than as they were thus preing to
gedyr suddenly there was a great cloud made in the air like a blaste of
thoundre and even there with the holy ghost come among hem Et apparnerunt illis
dispertite liugne tan quam ignis. And light come down among hem in likeness
of to^ges brennyng and not smertyng warmyng and not hermyng lyghtenyng and not
flateryng Et repletisu^t omnes spiritu sancto And fillid hem full of gostly
wit for as they where to sore but lewd men of sight and un let tered and
verray Ideottes as of co^yng and nothing cowde of clergy suddenly they were the
wyseste men and the best clerks in the world And anon they spoke all manner
langages under the son and there as before her hertis was cold for dread and
for fere of death Thanne were they so comfortid with the holy ghost in brennyng
love that they went and preached and taught the word of god sparyng for no
dread but ready to take the death for cristus sake Thanne at that time there
were in Iherusale^ people of all nations and drew in to the temple for great
fere of the blaste of thoundre that was in the air and stodyed what hit might
be.

Thanne come the posteles in to the temple and preached and all manner nations
vndirstode hem and they vndirstode all manner nations and so they p^chyd the
word of god Thanne were the people a stoyned wha^ they herd the posteles speak
all manner of langages. Than seyde sum these have drunk so much must that
they wotte not what they do seye nothir what they mean for they be all dronkyn
Than answerde petir and seyde we be not drunk but this was the prophecy of
Iohell the prophet how the holy ghost should be yeuen plenteuous to the people
so that they should speak with all tongues that is to p^che and all in the
worlds the law of criste.

Thanne the people tuened fast and so with in sewe yeris the seythe was in all
the world. Now hit is to wete why the holy ghost more apperyd in to likeness
of tongues rathir than in any other party of man's body and why he come to hem
sittyng rathir than standing. As to the fursce this is the cause. a tongue is
the best membre of a man's body when hit is in* good rewle and well disposed
but when hit is out of rewle hit is the worsce. Denenum aspidum sub labiis
eorum Bitter veneme is under the tongues that speakithe evil seythe David in
the sawter. And as seint Ieme seythe Acursed tongue is fired with fire of hell
and may not be chastifid while the fire brennyth hit And also for tongues must
speak wordis of fire that is sharp and sperkelyng to sey truth and notte
spare in prechyng and techyng to repreue mys dedis for as holy men in old time
overcome and drove a wey the fire of lyghtenyng with holy words and good
preyoures with the brennyng love to god right for the fire of the holy ghost
should drive a weye and overcome the fire of hell that envy has and evil
leuyng that regnyth now in the tongues of much people and in her heart And for
the apostlis and other prechoris that comythe aftyr hem should speak brennyng
wordis that is neythir to sharp nothir for dread nor for love to sey the
truth and to tell the people her defautes and to repreue the sin that
regneth in he^ in many diverse wise and so to do and sey the word of god and
to repreue sin. and but they woll leave sin they shall with out remedy be
damned in to the fire of hell for though thou shuldiste dye spare not to
preche the word of god and tell the truth Item deus e^ misericors
penitentibus pecca tasua. Also god is merciful to them that be sorry for her
sins and woll leave hem T^m uero confessus fuerit et relinuerit ea
misericordia co^se qua tur For though a man have do never so much sin and
he woll shreyue him and for sake his sin mercy shall follow him and he shall
have for yeuenesse and so come to the bryghte fire ever lastyng bliss that is
the precious love of god that brennythe among angelis and seyntis in heaven
Also he comythe in likeness of tongues of fire for it is the kind of fire to
make low that is high and to warm that is cold to make soft that is hard
and make hard that is soft And also the holy ghost makythe hertis that be
high of pride and envy he makythe hem low and warm in love and charity and
also hard hertis that have be gaderyng and holdyng of worldely goods the
holy ghost makythe hem soft and liberal to give and to de le alms deed
for the love of almighty god and makythe them hard also* in sufferyng of
hard and streyte leuyng and in doing of great penance for her sins. Thus
the holy ghost is ever ready to make salve ^or to hele all manner of sins

That other skylle is why the holy ghost come to the apostles rathir sittyng
thanne stondyng for sittyng be to kenythe meekness in heart with rest piece
and unity the which any m^ner a man must nedis have that woll ^^sceyue the
holy ghost for right ^s the dry wode wolle brenne clearly with onte steryng
so should every christian man love othyr with brennyng love and charity clearly
with out feynyng of wrath or envy or any manner of malice each with other and
every man should be f^yne of other is welfare and this ma^ythe to have a good
tongue. But as soon as the brondes be cast a twynne by desc^nsi^n of malice and
envy a none the fire of the holy ghost quenchith and thanne risithe up smoke
of great wrath and envy between party and party and also great greuaunce and
heaviness for the soul and causithe it to fail grace that it may have no
consideracion to reason than anon the wicked spirits been ready rise and up
smoke in the same man's heart that is for to say great wrath and envy and
evil will that hit may have no manner rest but ever stodyyng and thynkyng also
how he may avenge him and do vengeaunre un to his enemies and so is a man
ever tro^blid and besy in cursid ded is and like to be dampened body and soul
in hell to euerlasty^g p^yne but if he have socoure and help of the holy
gos^e and all soche things that may come of cursid and wicked tongues.

There for the holy ghost comythe in the likeness of tongues of fire to brenne
out the malice and envy and anoynte hem with sweetness of grace love and
charity. And therefore we shall prey to the holy ghost to give us grace so to
tempre our tongues that we may ever more speak good and that our hertys may be
fed with meekness that we may be abyll to be fed with the holy ghost. As
saint Gregor was when he expouned the prophecy he took to him his dekon
seint Petyr to write as he expouned. and made draw between him for petyr
schulde not se how he did in his stodyyngg. Thanne as Gregor satte in his
chair stodyyng holdyng up his hond^^ and his eyes to he uenward the holy ghost
come like a white down with foot and bill brennyng gold and satte on Gregor
right shu^dre and put her bill in Gregoris mouth. and when he with drew
it than he bad Petyr write and so continued till he had made an end. but he
expowned the gospel so boldly that Petyr had marvel there of and preuely
made an hole in the clothe y^ was between gregor and him and saw how the holy
ghost fed him. And a none the holy ghost show de Gr^gor how Petyr had done
Than Eregor blamyd Petyr and chargid him that he should never sey no thing
while he leued. But when gregor was deed an eretike would have bre^ned his
bokys that this holy man made and than Petyr with stood him and seyde nay and
told all how the holy ghost had done to him while he expowned the prophecy
and so sauyd his bokys vnbrennyd that he had made by the grace of god and
yifte of the holy ghost the which give us grace to be fed of him here in
our leuyng that we may have the bliss that never shall have end Amen.

In die s^ncte trinitatis


GOod men and wymmen this day is an high and a solemn feste in holy church
for it is of the holy Trinite For as holy church at wytsontyde makith mention
how the holy ghost come un to cristus disciples Now at this time is made
mention of all iij. pers^nes that is for to say. Pater filiue et spiritus Fadyr
and sone and holy ghost three persons and one god in trinite where for we be
bound to d^^ all the reverence and worship that we can or may to this holy
trinite Also ye shall understand why how and what the cause that this f^ste
was ordained

This holy feste was worshippid for the trinite fedyng for heretics
confoundyng and fore the trinite worshippyng Furste hitwas ordained for the
form of the trinite fyndyng And a great clerk Johan Bellet tellith that form
trinite was in the furste man ada^ onre form fadyr that come of the earth one
person and Eve of Adam the seconnde person of hem both come the iij.
persons as her child.

Thus the trinite was found in man where fore man should have mind to do
worship to the holy trinite. For holy church ordained that in weddyng of
man and woman to gedyr so that the mass of the trynyte is songon. and at his
death one belle shall be ronge in worshipp^ of the Trinite where for all
christian people be bound gretely to worship the holy Trinite. The secounde
cause is that feste is ordained in confoundyng of heretics and of lolleris for
to distroye them and their false opynyones that they had a yenste the holy
trinite fore right as he retikes in the be gynnyg of the feythe with her sweet
words and false opynynes where a boute to distroye the feythe of the holy
Trinite in the same wise lolleris now a days with her false spece of gyle be
a boute also to with draw the people from the true believe and feythe of the
holy trinite and the believe and feythe of holy church (...) marteres and
confessoures to the death Right so now this lolleris pursewithe men of holy church and be a boute in all manner weyes that they can and may find to
distroye and undo hem so that they might have her purpose. And thus they show
opynly that they be not godd is servants for they be out of charity and he
that is out of charity is fer from god but he that suffered tribulacion
persecucion and dissese fore the love of almyty god and prey for his enemies
and wolle not do no vengeance but put all in god almighty and he wolle quyte
hem full well in ever lasting bliss for our lord seyde thus. Michi vindictam
and ego retri^^am Put all thing to me and I shall quyte every man aftyr his
deseruyng for though god suffer holy church to be pursewid by soche mysse
and proud leueris but at the last he ordained soche a remedy that holy
church is holpyn and her enmyes con^undid and shamed. Thus it happid on a time
with the Emperor of Rome that hi ghte Attyl^ and he was made by heretics as
Johan bellet tellith the which Emperor pursewed Christian people sore and hatid
hem and holy church gretely. wherefor he made to do brenne all the bokys that
might be found of christian feythe. But as almighty god would there was a good
holy man and that was a great Clerk and that clerk was callid Alpynyons that
in meytenyng of the feyth of holy church he made the story of the Trynite and
the story also of seinte Stephyn and brought hit un to the pope for to have
hem songon and read in holy church But be counsel of that great clerk they
took the story of Seint stephyn and left the story of the holy Trinite till
to the time that Saint Gregory was pope than for to repreue hem and do hem
shame that be so the mysse beleuyng people and would not believe in the trinite
but made aftyr her reason many he retykes and in consideracion of hem seinte
Gregory the pope ordained this feste to be hallowed and this story to be songon
and radde in holy church in worship of the trinite with all criste^ people
The thride cause is for the high trinite worshippyng and fore all Christian men
should know how and in what manner they should believe in the trinite for as
holy church techithe he that beleuithe in the Trinite shall be saved and they
that does not shall be dampened. Thanne is it full expedyent and needful to
all Christian people to know how they shull leave. ye shall understand that
persite love to god is the believe for he that beleuith persitely makith no
questions that litill a vaylith. Fides non habet meritum vbi humana racio
prebet experimentu^. Feithe has no mede ne merit where man's wit yeuithe
experience. than is it good for all christian people to make love to be mediator
to the holy ghost prayng him to lyghton us with ynne our souls that we may
have grace to come to his persite believe There for this day was set next
with sunday hopyng that the holy ghost woll be ready to all Christian people that
woll call him and specially in lernyng of the feythe but yet for many wyttis
be doulle to learn tha^ they may not se nor here but they be brought in by
great ensample But that people is not most commendable if we may be ensample
come the sonner to the believe in the fadyr and the sone and the holy ghost iij.
persons and all one god take heed of this ensample Of yse snow and watyr how
that these iij. be diverse each in substance and yet is all but watyr. ye may
understand by the watyr the fadir by the yse the sone. and by the snow the
holy ghost watyr is an element that has great might and strength and as the
mastir Alysaundre seythe it is above heaven in the manner of yse like a cristall
and does worship to heaven and anon it is vudir earth and the earth is
grounded upon water And david seythe in the sauter it is all about the world
and in all thing for in hard stones and iron sum time sweet wa^^^ for this
watir is so full of (...)ghte is to understood (...)adir that his power is so
much that he gouernithe all the world. and knowith all thing and all is at
his will and commandment* By the sone Ihesu criste ye shall understood yse
that is water congelid hard and ^^^till that is ihesu criste verray god and
man that took the substance and fraye^te of mankind when he was conceived of
the holy ghost in the virgyn mary and borne of her body god that suffered
passion under pou^ce pilate done upon the cross dyed and was beryed and the
thridde day rose from death to lyffe and aftyr on holy thoursday styed up in
to heaven and shall come a yene at the day of dome and deem the quycke and the
deed. By the snow ye shall vndirstonde the holy ghost for right as snow is
but watir and yse and lihht^ in the air but how no man can tell So comythe the
holy ghost from the fadyr and the fone Spiritua sanctua a patre and filio non
factu^ nec creatu^ nec genitu^ sed proceden^ but how it is for no man to stody
for it excedit all men's wit to stody there upon. but sadly believe the
fadir is full god almighty. and of him come sone fulle god and of hem both
comythe the holy ghost full god. This trinite was known in the fullyng of
criste as the gospel tellithe. In baptismo christi tota trinitas se
manifestanit scilicet pater in ^oce fili^^ in carne spiritu^ sanctu^ in columba
et totum celum apertum erat. Than our lord ihesu criste was baptisid in the
watir of fli^ jordan and all the people nigh of the country there about were
baptized there with him and as they were in her preyoures Et aperti su^t celiet
spiritu^ sanctu^ descendit sicut columba. The holy ghost come down in
likeness of a white dove and lyghtyd on cristus head. Et vo^ de celo dice^^
Hic est fili^^ men^ dilect^^ in qno michi been complacni. And the fadir spoke
in heaven and said Thou art my well beloved sone that plesid me well that was
the holy Trinite that spoke in his person and the sone was there bodily in his
person when Johan baptiste seyde to the people Ecce agn^^ dei. Se the lombe
of god. and the holy ghost was seyne in his person. Sicut columba descendentem
as a white dove come down and these iij. be but one god in trinite wherefore
hit were full needful to all christian people to prey besely so that we may have
grace to have the persite love to believe in the fadir the sone and the holy
ghost three persons and one god^in trinite



we find that the modir of seynte Edmund^ of pounteney as he stody ed of this
holy Trinite she apperyd un to him and leyde in his honde^ iij rings each with
ynne o their. And in the furste was wreton Pater the fadir in the secounde
Filiua the sone and in the thride Spiritua sanctus. the holy ghost and seyde my
dear sone to soche figures take heed and learn what thou may and tak^ good
head to this ensample for right as a ring is round with out any be gynnyng
and endyng right so iij. persons in one god but for to stody how hit might be
it is but folly for hit exdithe any man's wit to mense there upon but saddely
believe there upon



we red of a clerk that was greatly learned in dyuynite the which stodyed
besely to have brought this in a book why god would be believed on god and three
persons and so as he walked on a day stodyyng in this matter by the sea sonde
he was ware of a fair child sittyng on the sea sonde and had a lytill
shelle in his hand and there with he took watyr out of the seeland cast hit
in to a litill pit fast Thanne seyde this mastir to this child sone what
doste y^ and he seyde Sire y am a boute to have all this watyr that is in the sea in to this litill pytte Than seyde this mastyr. that shalt thou never do
hit passithe any man's power. Sire seyde he as sone shall I do this as thou
shalt do that thou art a boute to do and anon the child vanishid a wey
Than this mastir thou ghte it was not goddis will and left his stodyyng in
that matter and thankythe god hyly By this ensample we may se that it is not
godd is will that we should mense in that matter but seedefastly believe in the
fadir the sone and the holy ghost Deni per fidem trinitati^ come by feythe and
love of this persite feythe of the trinite. Deni per opera miseri cordie come
by the werkys of mercy doing Deni per opera insticie come to this believe be
doing of werkys of right wisnesse and thus ye shall come to this per site
believe fadir and sone and holy ghost Et tu^c coronaberia corona glory eterne
And than thou shalt be crow ned with a crown of euerllastyng Joye and bliss
to the which bring us to the holy Trynite Amen

De corpore xp^^
GOod frendis ye shall understood that this das is an high and a solemn
feste in holy church the feste of corpus christi hit is the feste of our
lordis his own body the which is offered to the high fadir of heaven at the
auter in remission of our sins to all criste^ people that leave here in
persite lyffe and charity. and great socoure and help in releuyng hem that be
in peynes of purgatory there a bydyng the mercy of god ye shall understand
that this feste was found by a (...) that was callide v^bane the v* the which
had great grace and devotion in the sacrament in the Autee considering the
great me de help and socoure to man's soul and to the fortheryng of leuyng
to all christian people here in this present world there fore he ordained this
present feste to be hallowed in the next thoursday aftyr the feste of the holy
trinite for all criste^ people that wolle be saved must have ^adde believe in
the holy sacrament that hit is goddis own body in s^^me of bread made by ^^^
virtue of cristus word is that the priest seythe and by worchyng of the holy
ghost Thanne for this holy (...) thought to draw the people to more devotion
and bettir will to this holy sacrament and to do the service this day he
grauntith to all that be worthy that be tho that be verrey contrite and shreuyn
of her sins and be in the church at both euynsonges at matenesse and at
mass for each C. days of pardon and for each our of the day xl. days of
pardon and every day of the v^^s a C. days of pardon in remission of all her
sins for ever more enduryng Thanne ye shall understood that our lord (...)
crist on shereth ours day at night when he had souped and wyste well that
in the morrow that he should suffer passion and death and pass out of this
world vnt^ his fadir in heaven he ordained a perpetual memory of his passion
to a bide for ever with all christian people here in earth He took bread and wine
and made his own flesche and blood and yaue hit to his disciples to ete and to
drink and seyde Accipite et mandu cate hoc est corpna meum Take ye this and
ete hit for hit is mine own flesche and blood and this he deed for they should
have mind of him. And so he yafe to all other prestes power to make his own
body of bread and wine thus every priest has power to make the sacrament be he
good or badde for the sacrament may no man a mende nor a peyre but he that is a
good man and a holy lever helpith greatly tho that he preyith for And he that
does the office of the priest worthily and trewly. shall be glad and joyful
that ever he was borne. For owre lord has euine a priest a yefte and pour
here merth that he yafe neuyr to angelle in heuin that is to make his own body
in form of bread.

There fore e schall have worschipe more in heuyne thene any tongue can tell or
heart think and he that is an evil liffer and know is him self in dedely
sin and presumith to minister that worthi sacrament and woll note a mende
him he may be se were of perpetual damnacion with fyndis of hell in euyr
lasting pain.

Then schall e vndirsta^d that he grauntith this sacrament to be vsid for ever
more in holy church for four causes that be need full to all christian people
The first is for man's great helpyng. The second for cristus passion myndyng
The thridde for great ^one showing. And the fourth for great mede getyng. Nota
anod prop^er noue^ racio^es prodest homini a^dire miss^ secundum Angusti n^
Saint Austyn seith hit profitith greatly all christian people to here mass and in
special for ix. causi^ and seythe thus. Quia illo die qua audierat missam
necessaria cibaria et co^ced u^tur. For that day he herith a mass he shall
fail no bodily fode nor no necessary thing that shall be longyng to him nor
no let shall have in his iorneye where that ever he trauelithe The secounde
is all venial sins shall be for yeuen him and ydull word is The thridde is
if a man dy^ hit shall sconde for his ho sell The fourth he shall not that day
lose his sight The v. all ydull othis y^ day shall be for yeue^ him The vi.
that day he shall not dye no soden death. The vij. as long as he herith that
mass he shall not wex old. The viij. all his steppis toward and fromward the
church his good angel rekenythe to his salvation. The ix. all the while yt he
be holdithe the holy sacramental wikyd spirits fle from him and have no
power over him be he never so great a sinner. This help and so coure we have
of the holy ghost and of the sacrament here in earth and at our last end all
christian people woll send aftyr the priest to come to him with godd is body and
to reseyue hit knowing well that* he beleuyth stedefastly that it is the same
flesche and blood that criste took of our lady sinttmary and was borne of her
body verray god and man and aftyr suffered passion and death on the cross for
all mankind and leyde in tomb* And rose from death to live and now sittithe
on his faderis right hand in heaven and shall come a yene at the day of dome
and deem the quick and the deed every man aftir his deseruyng So this perfect
believe all christian people shall be armed and made strong to withsto^de the
fendes that wol come and a sail at the departing between the body and the
soul for tha^ne fendes come besely to bring him out of the believe. tha^ne
shall the sacrament that a man has resceyued in his lyffe make him mighty and
strong that he shall set all the fendes at naught and so over come hem. A
nothir skyll that the sacrament is brought to a man to ask mercy of criste
and remission of his sins having full trust and believe that criste is ever
ready to for give all them y^ woll ask mercy with ^ meke heart. As David
seythe. Cor contritu^ et bumiliatu^ deus non despicies A contrite heart and a
meke our lord shall never despise and that we may see ensample when he hunge
upon the cross between ij. theuys that were men of cursid leuyng And therefore
they where ordained to be deed and that one askid mercy with a meke heart ad
seyde Domine dum veneria in regnum tumn memento mei Lord quoth he when thon
comyste in to thy kingdom have mind on me and anon at his first askyng he
yaue him mercy and more over he said to him thus Hodie mecum eria in paradiso
This day thou shall be with me in paradise And that othyr theffewolde ask no
mercy in no wise for pride ^ he had in his heart and therefore he was dampened in
to hell. Thus our lord ^hesu criste shed his blood on the cross in health
to all mankind so in the mass every day he shewith his blood in great socour
help and salvation to all mankind and the same flescht and blood is shewid
every day in the mass for we should believe stedefastely there one And he yt
beleuyth not there on verily that it is so shall not be sauid at the day of dome.



Therefore I tell you this ensample that is in the lyffe of wode the bishope of
canterbury this bishop had with him clerkys that beleuyth not perfitly in the
sacrament of the auter and seyde they might not believe that the body and blood
of Criste might be ministret in the mass Thanne was this bishop sorry and
prayde to god besely for her amendment And so on a day when he was at the
mass and had made the fractione he saw the blood drope from the oste in to
the chalyse tha^ he made a sign un to he^ that believed not to come ne^^ him
and to se and wha^ they saw his fingeris blody and the blood ra^ne from the
oste in to the chalisse a none for great fere they cryde and seyde. O thou
blessid man that haste this grace to hold cristus body in thine hondis that
dropped blood in to the chalisse we believe verily there upon and we beseech the
to prey to him for us that thou haste in thy hondis that he take no vengeance
on us* for our missebeleue and we cry mekely mercy And a none the oste
turned in to the form of bread as hit was be fore and tha^ they were perfect
men of believe eueraftir Anothir skille is that the sacrament is made in the
Auter to make a man be oftyn sight there of the sooner to have mind on cristes
passion and to have it in mind for hit is the best defense a yenst tamptacion
of the fend. For seint Austyn seyth the mind of cristus passion puttith awey
all temptaciones and the power of all wickid spiritis And for this cause rodi^
and ymag ^ be set on high in the churches for as soon as a man comythe in to
the church he should se hit and have hit in his myde and think on cristus
passion where for crosses and other images be full necessary and needful. what
sum ever these ^ollers seyne for and hit had not be full profitable holy
faderis would have destroyed hem may yeris a gone. For right as the people do
worshipp^ to the kings seal not for lou^ of the seal but for reverence of the
king that it comythe fro So rodis and images be s^^^e for the kings seal of
heaven and other semtes in the same wise for Images belewde people is ^ok^^ And*
as ^ohan bellet seyth there be many thou sands of people that cannot ymagyn in
her h^^tis how criste was done on the cross but as they* se by images in
chirches and in other places theras they be And to have the betyr mind on
cristus passion I tell you this ensample



There was a christian man of England that went in to the holy lord and hired
an hethyn man to be his gyde and as he come in to a fair foreste and saw many
fair things but this christian man meruelyd gretely that he herd no noise of
byrddus and there of he had great marvel and seyde to this hethyn man I
marvel much that there is no song of byrddus in this wode than seyde this he
thyn man this is the woke that ye call passion woke that your great prophet
dyed y^^^ where for on sunday that last was that ye call palm sunday all the
fowls of this wode dye for sorrow and all this woke shall lie as deed But on
sunday next comyth that ye call Estyr day they quick a yene and all the year
aftyr make melodye. where for look up in to the trees and see and than he saw
every bow of the treeslye full of birdus as fladde as they had be sprede on
the cross Thanne sethe birddus have mind one cristus passion and make ^oche
morning and sorrow mo^h^ more cause has man kind that were boughte from ever
lastyng dampnacion to ever lastyng salvation by his passione

The thridde cause is why the sacrament is vsidin the auter for a man should by
the sight there of think on our lord ihe sulcriste fadyr of heuene that
has but oon sone that he louithe passing all thing but he sparid not to send
him down in to this world to suffer passion and death and to shede his
precious blood for ma^knde to by him out of the fendes bounds and to write a
chartour with his own precious blood of fredome for ever more to all man kind
so that a man forfete not his chartour by dedely sin but he that louithe god
woll keep his chartour for god askithe of a man but love where he seythe thus.
Damichi cor tuum et sufficit michi Sone give me thy heart and hit is y now for
me Thanne take heed of this ensample.



There was an Earl of venys was callid sire Ambryghte that louyd the sacrament
in the aut^r passing well and did hit all the worship and reverence that he
cowde and might. So when that he lay syke and should be deed he might not
resceyue the sacrament forcastyng than was he sorry and made dole and thaune he
let make clean his right side and to cover it with a fair clothe of sendell
and ley god dis body there on And said thus to the oste lord thou knowiste that
I love the with all my here and would feign resteyue the with my mouth and I
durst and therefore that I may notte I ley the on that place that is next to my
heart and so I show the all the love of my heart that I can and may where for
y beseech the good lord have mercy on me an^ even there with in sig^^ of all the
people that ^^^re about him his sydde opened and the Oste went there in to
his sydde And thanne his sydde closed a yene And soo^ none aftyr he did and
departid out of thi^ world So let us love the sacrament in our liffe and do
it reverence and worship and thanne at our last end wha^ we shall dye and
pass out of this world hit will socoure us and bring us to everlasting
bliss. Thus the sacrament is vsid for great mede getyng to all that believe
there ynne. for though it have the likeness of bread and the taste hit is
flesche and semythe bread it is quick and semythe deed ye mo^e believe verily
that it is goddis blessed body that took flesche and blood of the virgyne mary
and after did on the cross and rose from death to live and styed up in to
heaven and now sittithe on his faderis rigthe hand and shall come a yene at the
day of dome to deem the quick and the deed and he that resceyuith it here and
believed verily there upon shall have ever lastyng lyffe in the kingdom of heaven
as the gospel seythe.

Qui manducat hu^c pane^ viuet in eternum. Who so etith of this bread shall
leave ever and never be deed and he that resceyuith hit and beleuith not thus
Renaerit in iudicio at the day of dome he shall be dampened in to ever lastyng
pain. Augustinus in person^ xpristi. Manducas me non mutabis me inte sed ^n
mutabis in me. Seynte Austyn seythe in the person of criste Ete me but y shall
not turn and chance in to the but thou shalt turn and change in to me.

And thanne seyde christian man Dear nichil comedy For southe quod he I ete no

Thanne come a fair man that had many children in his armies. Et dedit
unicuique ue^irum unum pueru^^alem qua^e^ sacerdos ^^medit An^ yafeche criston
